"rd_so_tips_drone"		"IAF概要書:\n• ドローンの攻撃手段は爪だけです。部隊に接近する前に排除すれば被害は受けません。\n• 一部のドローンは長距離を跳躍することがわかっています。\n　爆発性の武器を使用する場合は、ターゲットが素早く自分も巻き込む範囲に寄ってくる可能性があるので、\n　細心の注意を払いましょう。\n• ドローンは配管を通ったり足場の下から這い出てくることもあります。\n　その様なドローンの出現地点を塞ぐことで海兵隊への攻撃ができない場所に閉じ込めておくことも、\n　場合によっては可能です。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_drone"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Drones only attack with their claws. Taking them out before they reach the squad will render them harmless.\n• Certain drones have been known to leap large distances. Take extra precautions when using explosive weaponry, as targets may rapidly advance into unsafe range.\n• Drones can crawl through ducts and under scaffolding. It is sometimes possible to block the drones' points of egress, trapping them in a location where they are not a threat to marines."
"rd_so_tips_ranger"		"IAF概要書:\n• レンジャーの酸性攻撃は一定の高さで飛びます。ドッジロールで転がり抜けることで完全に回避できます。\n• レンジャーには近接攻撃手段がありません。接近した場合のリスクは酸弾のゼロ距離射撃だけです。\n• レンジャーは発射準備中に向きを変えることが出来ません。\n　そのスキを利用して側面を取ったり近接攻撃範囲内に潜り込みましょう。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_ranger"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The ranger's acidic weapon travels at a constant height. Dodge roll out of the way for a clean escape.\n• Rangers lack a melee attack. The only risk in getting close to a ranger is a point-blank acid orb.\n• Rangers cannot turn while firing. Use this opportunity to flank or get into melee range."
"rd_so_tips_shieldbug"		"IAF概要書:\n• シールドバグの前面にある巨大な骨の層は完全に無敵です。\n　側面や隙間から攻撃することでダメージを与えられます。\n• シールドバグには2種類の構えがあります。\n　「攻撃」モードでは高速で移動と旋回をする代わりに、骨の層による防御範囲が小さくなります。\n　「防御」モードでは移動と旋回が遅くなる代わりに防御を固めます。\n• シールドバグは攻撃されると多くの場合は防御モードに切り替わります。\n　多くの場合は一度撃って動きを遅くすることで側面からの攻撃をしやすくするのが最適な戦術となります。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_shieldbug"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The large bone plates on the front of a shieldbug are completely invulnerable. Attack from the side or through gaps to do damage.\n• Shieldbugs have two stances. The \"offensive\" stance moves and turns faster, but reduces coverage from the bone plates. The \"defensive\" stance moves and turns slower in exchange for having its shields up.\n• Shieldbugs often switch to defensive stance when injured. It's often best to shoot one before attempting to flank to take advantage of its reduced movement speeds."
"rd_so_tips_boomer"		"IAF概要書:\n• ブーマーを怒らせると爆発する。膨張するのを見たら、破裂した後の光る塊を避けた方が良いでしょう。\n• ブーマーの危険性は主に破裂することにありますが、近づきすぎると蹴り飛ばそうともしてきます。\n• ブーマーは壁の下から現れたり床を転がって海兵隊を驚かすことでも知られています。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_boomer"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Boomers explode when provoked. If you see one inflating, it's wise to avoid the glowing blobs after it bursts.\n• Boomers are mainly dangerous because they burst, but they may attempt to kick you if you get too close.\n• Boomers are known to emerge from under walls or roll across the floor to menace marines."
"rd_so_tips_buzzer"		"IAF概要書:\n• バザーの主な攻撃方法は撹乱です。\n　バザーの攻撃により重大な場面で海兵隊の視界が数秒でも重要な瞬間に遮られてしまうこともあります。\n• バザーは小さく、素早く、空を飛んでいます。そのせいで実弾系の武器で狙うのは困難であり、\n　経験豊富な海兵隊は近接攻撃の方が「ハエ叩き」しやすいと判断している場合が多いです。\n• バザーは比較的小さいダメージしか与えませんが、放っておくと命に関わる事になります。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_buzzer"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The buzzer's main weapon is distraction. Their attack can disrupt a marine's vision for a few precious seconds at a crucial moment.\n• Buzzers are small, quick, and airborne. This makes them a challenge for projectile-based weapons - wise marines often find it easier to \"swat the flies\" with melee attacks.\n• Buzzers deal relatively little damage, but if left unchecked, they can be deadly."
"rd_so_tips_parasite"		"IAF概要書:\n• パラサイトは人間の頭部を利用して増殖します。\n　海兵隊がパラサイトに組み付かれたら、爆発して多くのパラサイトをバラ撒く前に素早く治療する必要があります。\n• 帯電アーマーは海兵隊の頭に取り付いたパラサイトを除去できる医療以外で唯一の手段です。\n　パラサイト自身でも卵の状態でも、炎を浴びせれば繁殖活動を開始できなくさせられます。\n• 寄生された海兵隊は視界が赤くなるという報告がされています。\n　治療が不可能なら、肉体を苗床にされる前に仲間の手で死なせてあげるのが賢明で慈悲深い選択です。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_parasite"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Parasites reproduce with the help of human heads. If a parasite latches onto a marine, prompt medical attention is required to keep them from exploding into more parasites.\n• Electrified armor is the only non-medical way to prevent parasites from coupling with a marine's head once they attach. Fire, applied either to the parasite itself or the egg, will render the specimen infertile and unable to initiate the process.\n• Infested marines report their vision turning red. If medical care is unavailable, the wise and merciful option is to put them down with friendly fire before their body can be used to scatter more parasites."
"rd_so_tips_mortarbug"		"IAF概要書:\n• モルタルバグは巨大で強力なレンジャーです。\n　余裕がある隊員は壁越しに飛んでくる砲撃を見落とさないようにしましょう。\n• モルタルバグは酸ではなく、一定時間後に爆発する爆弾を吐き出します。\n• モルタルバグの爆弾はエイリアンにも海兵隊にもダメージを与えます。\n　俊敏な隊員ならそれを利用して密集したエイリアン相手に優位に立ち回れます。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_mortarbug"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Mortarbugs are larger, stronger rangers. Capable marines keep an eye out for mortar shots coming over walls.\n• Instead of acid, mortarbugs spit bombs that explode after a constant length of time.\n• Mortarbug bombs are capable of damaging aliens and marines alike. Swift marines can take advantage of this to help clear densely-packed swarms."
"rd_so_tips_harvester"		"IAF概要書:\n• ハーベスターは直接の攻撃はせず、代わりにゼノマイトを産み出して攻撃させます。\n• 海兵隊はハーベスターに近づく際には注意すべきです。\n　直接攻撃はしてこないけれど、皮膚が腐食性で触れるのは危険です。\n• ハーベスターは様々なエイリアンの中で海兵隊から離れようと動く数少ない一種です。\n　ゼノマイトの群衆が押し寄せるのを止めるためにハーベスターを追いかけなければならなくなることもあります。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_harvester"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Instead of attacking directly, harvesters spawn xenomites to attack for them.\n• Marines should exercise caution when approaching a Harvester. They don't attack directly, but their skin is corrosive.\n• Harvesters are one of the few known specimens that will walk away from marines. You may have to chase them down to stem the tide of xenomites."
"rd_so_tips_xenomite"		"IAF概要書:\n• ゼノマイト唯一の危険な点は背中の酸袋です。\n• ゼノマイトは海兵隊に飛びついて自爆しようとします。\n　海兵隊はゼノマイトを先に殺してしまえば身を守ることができます。\n• ゼノマイトが居るのは基本的に近くにハーベスターが居る兆候ですが、単独で居る場合もあります。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_xenomite"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The only dangerous part of a xenomite is the acid sac on its behind.\n• Xenomites will attempt to jump onto marines and detonate themselves. Marines can refuse xenomites by killing them first.\n• Xenomites often indicate that a Harvester is nearby, but they're also known to exist independently."
"rd_so_tips_mender"		"IAF概要書:\n• メンダーは伸縮する赤緑の舌を使うことで、仲間のエイリアンを治療する能力を持っています。\n　賢い海兵隊ならこれに対処しない限り状況の悪化を止めるのは難しいとわかるはずです。\n• メンダーは他のエイリアンよりかなり珍しい種族です。\n　大抵の新兵はメンダーとの初遭遇で慌てて、貴重な弾薬をすぐ治る傷をつけるだけのために浪費しがちです。\n• メンダーは危険な状況になると一度逃げ出して状況を立て直そうとすることがわかっています。\n　その機会を与えないように妨害しましょう。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_mender"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The mender is capable of healing its fellow aliens with its stretchy, red and green tongue. Wise marines will find it difficult to stem the tide until it's dealt with.\n• Menders are considerably rarer than other alien species. Novice marines often panic their first time seeing one and waste precious ammunition causing quickly-healed wounds.\n• Menders are known to run away and regroup when the going gets tough. Cut them off before they get the chance."
"rd_so_tips_biomass"		"IAF概要書:\n• バイオマスはエイリアンの生命サイクルの中で何らかの役割を果たしていると思われます。\n　直接攻撃はしてこないが、触れた物を溶かします。\n• バイオマスを排除する唯一の手段は焼き払うことです。\n　海兵隊は火を使うか多少の被害を受けながら近くを通るかを判断しなければなりません。\n• 全てではないけれど、一部のバイオマスは燃やされるとエイリアンの群れを呼ぶフェロモンを放出します。\n　見慣れないバイオマスに点火する際には戦闘準備をしておきましょう。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_biomass"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Biomass is thought to fill a role in the alien life cycle. It cannot attack directly, but it is corrosive to the touch.\n• The only way to actually eliminate a biomass is to burn it off. Marines have to consider whether to bring fire or simply accept some damage to cross.\n• Some, but not all, biomass releases pheromones that call in a swarm when burned. Be prepared to fight when lighting unfamiliar biomass."
"rd_so_tips_grub"		"IAF概要書:\n• グラブは攻撃手段を持たず体力も僅かしかありません。踏むだけで殺せます。\n• グラブがいる場所には確実ではありませんが、パラサイトがいる事が多いです。\n　この事を知る海兵隊なら予め注意することで有利に立ち回れるでしょう。\n• 踏みつけに対してグラブが持つ唯一の自己防衛手段は壁を登れるという点だけです。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_grub"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Grubs have no weapons and very little health. They can be killed simply by stepping on them.\n• Parasites are often, but not always, nearby when grubs are present. Capable marines take advantage of this early warning.\n• A grub's only natural defense against boots is their ability to climb walls."

// "Space Series" is a joke on how the big baseball championship in the United States and Canada is called the "World Series".
// "Bosco" is named after a friend's cat, but I think the cat is named after a brand of chocolate syrup. No jokes or plot depends on this, so feel free to leave it as is or replace it with a cat/food/etc. you like
// "Basebees" is a portmanteau of "baseball" and "bees" because they're baseball-shaped bees.
// in the game of baseball, a runner is "tagged out" if a player on the opposing team touches them with the baseball before they can reach a base. doing this means they must stop running and are "out". (but tagging them with something else, like an empty glove or a bee, does nothing.)
// to explain "fielding all the pieces": in the game of baseball, after the batter hits the ball, they will run around the bases. if the batter hits the ball hard enough (and in the right direction), it will land in the outfield. The outfield is between the bases and the edge of the field where the spectator seats are. It's the "outfield" because it's the outer part of the field. Anyways, the job of the outfielders is to stand in the outfield, catch any balls that are hit their way, and throw those balls to their teammates on first, second, third, and home base so that they can tag the runner out. (This is a simplification of the actual rules, but it will hopefully suffice.) This process of catching the ball and throwing it where it needs to be is called "fielding". A player that successfully catches and throws the ball where it needs to go is a "good fielder". In this case, this is difficult to do with an exploded ball because you have to catch all the pieces and tag the runner with all of them! This might be able to be simplified to "you have to catch all the pieces" or something.
// regarding "mercy rule": https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mercy_rule
// the last line is a play on the American English idiom "It's not whether you win or lose, it's how you play the game." It was originally said about baseball, but it's often applied to every sport and, really, any other endeavor. It's typically said to emphasize the importance of sportsmanship (playing fair, losing gracefully, etc.)
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_mortarbug_4"		"03/28/53, 18:52\nWell, today was the big Space Series championship. Big Report pitched, of course, for the Upper Deck Robust Rookies against the Lower Deck Bosco Orbs. True to their name, the Orbs managed to genetically engineer some ball-shaped basebees to play outfield. I think they heard we had an insect player and refused to be outdone. The bees are not as effective as you might think - they find it hard to lift the gloves and put them in the way of the ball, even if they can fly. They mainly affect the game by being about the same shape as a baseball, so you gotta make sure you're getting tagged out by the right orb. If you get tagged out by a bee, you can keep running! I did manage to get Big Report spitting baseballs before the big game, even if they are covered in a thin layer of time bomb juice. This usually led to the balls either going off in the catcher's mitt (relatively harmless once we armored the glove) or exploding in midair after the hit. Very pretty, but it turns out that if the ball explodes, you have to field all the pieces. Long story short, the mercy rule made us call the game once we were losing 68 to 1. I still count it as a success. It's not whether you win or lose, it's how you taught a bomb-spitting space bug to play the game."

// to strip wire means to remove the insulating plastic coat so it's just bare copper or whatever metal is inside.

// "we did surgery on a bug" is a riff on "they did surgery on a grape", a meme from a few years ago.
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_1"		"I am here to spill the beans on these oft-maligned creatures. Yes, their headbutts can be a pain, but they can be quite lovely in the right light. If you're lucky enough to see one while the sunset shimmers, I find the chitin shines quite beautifully in the twilight. Sparkle aside, it's quite tough and useful for a number of military and industrial purposes. The hard part is separating it from the rest of the antlion. We've had some luck with crowbars, but several colleagues have suggested simply cutting the softer flesh away. I don't see any reason why this wouldn't work, but I'd like to verify it myself before someone loses a finger. I'd hate for someone to lose a pinkie to some pie in the sky idea about antlion surgery. I would much prefer to have good news if we did surgery on a bug!"
"rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_2"		"今後の研究用に生きた検体を確保しているのを見ました。素晴らしい！こいつらは魅力的な生物で、やるべき事はたくさんあります。こいつらの解凍は必ず完全にコントロール下にある研究環境内で行うということを留意しておいて下さい。経験則から言うと、アントライオンを輸送する際には、容器を室温より約20%クールにすべきです。我々は何度か失敗をしましたが、全ては正しくない輸送・保管方法の結果起きた防げるはずの死傷事故で、最善な手法を明確にしていない点と器具の不備のせいだと断言します。"
// "it needs to be about twenty percent cooler" is an ancient, popular My Little Pony joke that comes from this clip: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=L83cTan6ESk It was popular enough that it's been turned into songs, t-shirts, and other media, but that clip is the original.
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_2"		"I've seen some of you taking live specimens for further study. Good! They're fascinating creatures and there's a lot of work to be done. Do note that you should only thaw them out under controlled laboratory conditions. A good rule of thumb is that, when transporting an antlion, the container needs to be about twenty percent cooler than room temperature. We've had a number of unfortunate, all-too-preventable casualties result from improper transportation and storage, and I blame the lack of clear best practices and inadequate equipment."
"rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_3"		"それの解消を目標として、現在は重粒子振動阻害移送システムを開発中でして、初期段階の報告では完成可能な見込みがあるとお知らせできたことを嬉しく思います。これは重粒子変換器とアントライオンガードより少しだけ大きい拘束用の檻でできています。亜原子粒子振動を操作する事で、変換器が一瞬で檻を摂氏5度近くまで下げることができ、エネルギーを少ししか消費せずにその温度変化を維持することが可能です。冷気は檻の中のアントライオンのエネルギーも急速に奪うので、壁面は最低限の強度で大丈夫です。これだけで車輪付き冷蔵庫としか言えない馬バスよりもアントライオンの移送がとても容易になります！残りのテストに合格できたら、これを通称『長靴を履いたウマ』として運用したいです。その時がこの魅力的な生物についてもっと安全に研究しようと頑張った我々の大勝利と言えましょう。"
// "Baryon Oscillation Obstructive Transport System" and "baryonic transducer" are arbitrary technobabble as setup for the rest of the paragraph. Feel free to change it as needed. This is hard to explain, but the short version is "a horse sitting in a boot and saying 'love wins' is an inside joke". It started by putting an emoji of a horse head (originally Graceful Spark's) over the boot emoji and noticing that they fit well together, and it grew from there.
// "horse truck" is used here as "a machine you use to move horses around" and as a reference to the above My Little Pony podcast, "We Were Hit By A Horse Truck And Got Isekai'd Into Equestria?".
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_3"		"To this end, we're developing the Baryon Oscillation Obstructive Transport System, and I'm pleased to announce that early reports look promising. It consists of a baryonic transducer and a holding cell scarcely larger than an antlion guard. By manipulating subatomic vibrations, the transducer instantly cools the cage by approximately five degrees Celsius and maintains that temperature gradient indefinitely with very little additional energy required. Since the cold rapidly saps a captured antlion's energy, the walls only require minimal reinforcement. This alone makes them much easier to move around than the old freezer-on-wheels horse truck design! If our remaining tests pass, I will recommend we begin keeping these so-called horses in BOOTS. That would be a lovely win for all of us trying to safely learn more about these fascinating creatures."
"rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_4"		"アントライオン達を相手にする時は注意しろとは絶対に言わなきゃいけませんし、アントライオンガードも例外ではありません。あいつらは見張っている時に軽快に走り回るなんてことは滅多に無いし、恥ずかしがり屋なペガサスのように飛び回ることも無いでしょう。でも突然突進して押し倒してきて、そうなったら相手が死ぬまでそれを止めません。我々が踏み込んでいるのは未知の領域であることは忘れがちですし、まだまだわからないことが多すぎます。人類の研究史の限界を押し上げ新世界への光を灯すのは一筋縄ではいきませんが、注意力と責任感を臨めばリスクは最小限にすることができます。このチャンスについてよく考えて下さい。"
// "light on their pointy little legs" is a riff on "light on their feet", which is an idiom for someone who is agile or nimble.
// Fluttershy is another pony.
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_4"		"I must urge caution when dealing with antlions, and the guards are no exception. They are hardly light on their pointy little legs and will not flutter shyly by while you watch. They will charge you, knock you down, and make themselves a problem until one of you dies. It's easy to forget that we're in uncharted territory here and there's so much we still don't know. Pushing boundaries and illuminating new frontiers of human knowledge is never easy or safe, but the risk can be minimized if we're careful and only take responsible, considered chances."
"rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_5"		"簡単な話にまとめますと、アントライオンの飼育研究は順調です。アントライオンとの間の上下関係をフェロモン腺を使って操作することで研究は飛躍的に進歩を遂げましたが、アントライオンガードには効きませんでした。この事の解決のために、果物と野菜を使用したら非常に上手くいきました。あいつらは頑固な石頭ですがアップルとジャックフルーツが大好きで、たまにはウリ類も食べています。中身の違う偽物のカボチャも与えてみましたが、これには苛立っていたようでした。反省しなければいけませんね。満ち足りた虫は幸福な虫で、幸福な虫は無意味に人を襲うことが滅多に無くなるということは憶えておいて下さい。愛情を頭突きで表現するので、もう一度言っておきますと、必ず注意と対策をしておいて下さいね。お忙しい中のご清聴まことにありがとうございました。私は信じております。いつか時期が来れば、この生物たちを家畜化する方法は見つかると。不和と混沌を取り除き魔法のようにトモダチになれる力、それは我々の手の中にあるのです！"
// "apples, jackfruit" is a reference to the pony Applejack.
// the watermelon full of fruit is a reference to the practice of stuffing pumpkins with raw meat to provide enrichment for captive tigers. https://carolinatigerrescue.org/newsroom/pumpkin-enrichment/
// the Elements of Harmony are the magic jewelry (and the associated personality traits) that allow the main characters of My Little Pony: Friendship is Magic to laser blast their enemies. Discord is one villain they defeated this way.
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_antlionguard_5"		"To end on a lighter note, our research into proper antlion care and feeding has been going brilliantly. We've made good strides manipulating other antlion castes with pheropods, but that doesn't work with the guards. To that end, we've had quite some success with fruit and vegetables. They're quite fond of apples, jackfruit, and the occasional gourd. We've begun giving our captive antlions hollowed-out watermelons filled with other food, and they seem to enjoy the challenge! Remember, an enriched bug is a happy bug and a happy bug is far less likely to hurt someone on purpose. They do show affection through headbutts, so, once again, due caution and preparation are advised. Thank you for your time and attention, and I have faith that, in due time, we will find a way to keep these creatures docile in captivity. The elements of harmony, or at least the lack of discord, are within our grasp!"
